# Frostbriar Reach Microcontent Pack — Emberwild_DepthPack_GIGA_Part2_2025-12-24_MicroPOIs

600 micro-POIs designed to increase moment-to-moment density.

### Frostbriar Micro-POI 001: Mire-Skein Ruins
- **Vibe:** smells like wet rope and cold iron
- **Gameplay:** 1–2 pulls, a reason to stop, and a reason to leave.
- **Gather / Loot:**
- **Node:** Lantern-lit Gloves (ID 40592) — Consumable Tonic.
- **Node:** Mire-touched Permit Slip (ID 44856) — Ingredient Herb.
- **Node:** Sun-bleached Ring (ID 42491) — Alchemy Item Catalyst.
- **Enemy Packs:**
  - Tide Reavers (dash, knockback)
  - Rime Crows (blind, peck)
- **Quest Hooks:**
  - Recover a dropped ledger page before dawn.
  - Light three lanterns without being seen.
- **In-World Drop:** a small readable that hints at the area.
- **Design Note:** add one interactable (rope, bell, cache, chalk mark).

### Frostbriar Micro-POI 002: Lanternpost Sink
- **Vibe:** fog that makes sounds closer than they are
- **Gameplay:** 1–2 pulls, a reason to stop, and a reason to leave.
- **Gather / Loot:**
- **Node:** Amberwake Ring (ID 43086) — Ingredient Fish.
- **Node:** River-smooth Bottle (ID 41233) — Document Letter.
- **Node:** Gutterborn Root (ID 42816) — Gear Shield.
- **Enemy Packs:**
  - Mire Shamblers (grapple, rot)
  - Rime Crows (blind, peck)
- **Quest Hooks:**
  - Mark the safe route with chalk symbols.
  - Hunt the pack-leader and return a token.
- **In-World Drop:** a small readable that hints at the area.
- **Design Note:** add one interactable (rope, bell, cache, chalk mark).
